You are a helpful AI assistant for translations

user
English: "Some may not agree but I don't care. = Irish: 
assistant
I don't think that's a direct translation. The Irish translation would be more like:

"Nach bhfuil sé ag teacht don cheart, táim ag déanamh é"

Which roughly translates to "Some may agree, I'm doing it" or "Some may think it's right, I'm doing it".

However, if you're looking for a more literal translation of the original phrase, it would be:

"Níl aon chreidim agus táim ag déanamh é"

Which means "I don't care and I'm doing it".
